<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Results of Operations and Financial Condition </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&#160;28, 2023, iCAD, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its financial results for the quarter and year ended December&#160;31, 2022. A copy of the Company&#8217;s press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>iCAD Reports Financial Results for Fourth Quarter ended December&nbsp;31, 2022 and Year End </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Strategy focused on profitability by end of 2024, using current cash on hand </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>New leadership to host conference call and webcast today at 4:30 PM ET </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NASHUA, N.H. </B>&#150;<B> March</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;28, 2023 </B>&#150; iCAD, Inc. (NASDAQ: ICAD),&nbsp;a global medical technology leader providing
innovative cancer detection and therapy solutions, today reported its financial and operating results for the twelve months ended December&nbsp;31, 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Highlights: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company continues to invest in Detection business, driving commercial growth through global adoption of Breast AI
Suite while exploring strategic options for Therapy segment </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Several strategic partnership agreements signed in Q4, including Google Health and Solis Mammography, positioning
the Company for growth </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Promising clinical research reaffirms clinical value and utility of Breast AI Suite </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company reduces annualized expenses by $4.3 to $4.6&nbsp;million and decreases annualized cash burn by $4.9 to
$5.2&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;In the battle against cancer, we see early detection and diagnosis as a key part in transforming the patient
journey and quality of care. Breast cancer is the most common cancer in women worldwide and the second leading cause of cancer death among women in the U.S. With iCAD&#146;s early detection technology, we have the ability to detect cancers early,
giving individuals the opportunity for more positive outcomes and more lives saved. The body of evidence supporting our Breast AI suite continues to grow, and we are committed to upholding our vision to be the world&#146;s most pervasive and
personalized suite of AI cancer detection solutions. We look forward to strengthening our focus to rapidly advance our progress in this area,&#148; said Dana Brown, President and CEO of iCAD, Inc. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We are amidst an exciting period of transition across many aspects of the Company, including the shift to a partnership approach for both select
elements of our business as well as our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">go-to-market</FONT></FONT> strategy. Several key partnerships and agreements were signed in Q4, including a strategic development and
commercialization agreement with Google Health, which is positioned to improve our market-leading AI solutions for mammography, expand access to our technology to millions of women and providers worldwide, and accelerate time to market for our own
cloud-based SaaS solution planned for 2024. We are also continuing to strengthen our partnership with Solis Mammography, the largest independent provider of breast screening and diagnostic services in the U.S. We remain enthusiastic about the
potential these partnerships present in 2023 and beyond,&#148; said Ms.&nbsp;Brown. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;While both the Therapy and Detection lines of business have
significant market opportunity and potential, we believe our core competencies and focus need to be solely on Detection and our strategy around AI. We remain confident that the Xoft technology has the potential to positively impact the lives of
cancer patients and the providers who care for them on a global scale. As we move through this time of transition, we want to explore strategic options that could accelerate the accessibility of this technology and provide more focus and synergies
to its growth. As we explore these opportunities, we are projecting to be cash flow positive and reach profitability before the end of 2024. We believe these changes give us the runway needed to successfully navigate this business model transition
without needing to raise additional capital,&#148; said Ms.&nbsp;Brown. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total Detection and Therapy revenue for the&nbsp;fourth quarter of 2022 was $6.5&nbsp;million, a decrease of $1.3&nbsp;million, or 17%, as compared to the
fourth quarter of 2021. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$5.7&nbsp;million, or 73% of revenue, in the fourth quarter of 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the fourth quarter of 2022 were
$8.0&nbsp;million, a 19% decrease from $9.9&nbsp;million in the fourth quarter of 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP Net Loss: Net loss for the fourth quarter of 2022 was ($3.1)
million, or ($0.12) per diluted share, as compared to a net loss of ($4.1) million, or ($0.17) per diluted share, for the fourth quarter of 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss, a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the fourth quarter of 2022 was ($3.0) million, or ($0.12) per diluted share, as compared to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss of
($4.1) million, or ($0.17) per diluted share, for the fourth quarter of 2021. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the
accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss results for the three-month periods ended December&nbsp;31, 2022 and 2021,
respectively. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the Twelve months ended December&nbsp;31, months ended December&nbsp;31, 2022 were $33.7&nbsp;million, as
compared to $35.0&nbsp;million in the Twelve months ended December&nbsp;31, months ended December&nbsp;31, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP Net Loss: Net loss for the Twelve
months ended December&nbsp;31, months ended December&nbsp;31, 2022 was ($13.7) million, or ($0.54) per diluted share, as compared to a net loss of ($11.21) million, or ($0.45) per diluted share, for the Twelve months ended December&nbsp;31, months
ended December&nbsp;31, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss:
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the Twelve months ended December&nbsp;31, months ended December&nbsp;31, 2022 was ($13.6)
million, or ($0.54) per diluted share, as compared to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss of ($10.7) million, or ($0.43) per diluted share, for the Twelve months ended December&nbsp;31, months ended December&nbsp;31,
2021. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a
reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss results for the twelve-month periods ended December&nbsp;31, 2022 and 2021, respectively. </P>

loss of ($11.7) million, a $4.4&nbsp;million increase as compared to the&nbsp;Twelve months ended December&nbsp;31, months ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA loss of ($7.3) million. Please
refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP
Measures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company reports its financial results in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles, or GAAP. However,
management believes that in order to understand the Company&#146;s short-term and long-term financial and operational trends, investors may wish to consider the impact of certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> or <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items, when used as a supplement to financial performance measures in accordance with GAAP. These items result from facts and circumstances that vary in frequency and/or impact on continuing
operations. Management also uses results of operations before such items to evaluate the operating performance of the Company and compare it against past periods, make operating decisions, and serve as a basis for strategic planning. These <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide management with additional means to understand and evaluate the operating results and trends in the Company&#146;s ongoing business by eliminating certain <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses and other items that management believes might otherwise make comparisons of the Company&#146;s ongoing business with prior periods more difficult, obscure trends in ongoing operations or reduce
management&#146;s ability to make useful forecasts. Management believes that these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide additional means of evaluating period-over-period operating performance. In addition,
management understands that some investors and financial analysts find this information helpful in analyzing the Company&#146;s financial and operational performance and comparing this performance to its peers and competitors. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management defines <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA&#148; as the sum of GAAP Net Loss before provisions for interest
expense, other income, stock-based compensation expense, depreciation and amortization, tax expense, severance, gain on sale of assets, loss on disposal of assets, acquisition and litigation related expenses. Management considers this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to be an indicator of the Company&#146;s operational strength and performance of its business and a good measure of its historical operating trends, in particular the extent to which
ongoing operations impact the Company&#146;s overall financial performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures do
not replace the presentation of the Company&#146;s GAAP financial results and should only be used as a supplement to, not as a substitute for, the Company&#146;s financial results presented in accordance with GAAP. The Company has provided a
reconciliation of each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure used in its financial reporting and investor presentations to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management excludes each of the items identified below from the applicable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure referenced above
for the reasons set forth with respect to that excluded item: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Interest expense: The Company excludes interest expense which includes interest from the facility agreement,
interest on capital leases and interest on the convertible debentures from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA calculation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Stock-based compensation expense: excluded as these are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses
that management does not consider part of ongoing operating results when assessing the performance of the Company&#146;s business, and also because the total amount of expense is partially outside of the Company&#146;s control as it is based on
factors such as stock price volatility and interest rates, which may be unrelated to our performance during the period in which the expense is incurred. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Amortization and Depreciation: Purchased assets and intangibles are amortized over a period of several years and
generally cannot be changed or influenced by management after they are acquired. Accordingly, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items are not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that
such expenses do not have a direct correlation to future business operations. Thus, including such charges does not accurately reflect the performance of the Company&#146;s ongoing operations for the period in which such charges are incurred.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Loss on fair value of convertible debentures. The Company excludes this
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> item as it is not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such item does not have a direct correlation to future business operations.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Litigation related: These expenses consist primarily of settlement, legal and other professional fees related to
litigation. The Company excludes these costs from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures primarily because the Company believes that these costs have no direct correlation to the core operations of the Company.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Loss on extinguishment of debt: The Company excludes this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> item
as it is not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such item does not have a direct correlation to future business operations. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On occasion in the future, there may be other items, such as loss on extinguishment of debt, significant asset impairments, restructuring charges or
significant gains or losses from contingencies that the Company may exclude if it believes that doing so is consistent with the goal of providing useful information to investors and management. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Set forth below is a reconciliation of the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA&#148; </P>
